mysql> SELECT release_year, AVG(rating_score) AS avg_rating
    -> FROM (
    ->     SELECT release_year,
    ->     CASE rating
    ->         WHEN 'G' THEN 1
    ->         WHEN 'PG' THEN 2
    ->         WHEN 'PG-13' THEN 3
    ->         WHEN 'R' THEN 4
    ->         -- Add other mappings here
    ->         ELSE NULL
    ->     END AS rating_score
    ->     FROM netflix
    ->     WHERE rating IS NOT NULL AND rating != ''
    -> ) AS ratings
    -> GROUP BY release_year
    -> ORDER BY release_year;
